lazy={
    addListener:function(type,fn){
        if (this.addEventListener){this.addEventListener(type, fn, false);
        }else {this.attachEvent('on' + type, fn);}
    },
    removeListener:function(type, fn){
        if (this.removeEventListener) this.removeEventListener(type, fn, false);
        else this.detachEvent('on' + type, fn);
    },
    preventDefault:function(){
        this.preventDefault?this.preventDefault():this.returnValue=false;
    },
    init:function(){
        var _this=this;
        this.addListener.call(document.body,'click',function(e){
            e=e||window.event;
            var target=e.target||e.srcElement;
            if('A'===target.tagName && target.href.test(/-?(login\.html)|(signup\.html)/)){
            _this.preventDefault.call(e);
            if(!window.lazyload)
            window.lazyload=target.href.test(/-?login\.html/)?1:2;
        }
        _this.removeListener.call(document.body,'click',arguments.callee);
    });
}
};

var $_GET = (function(){
    var url = window.document.location.href.toString();
    var u = url.split("?");
    if(typeof(u[1]) == "string"){
        u = u[1].split("&");
        var get = {};
        for(i=0;i<u.length;i++){
            var j = u[i].split("=");
            get[j[0]] = j[1];
        }
        return get;
    } else {
        return {};
    }
})();
var getHost = function(url) {
    var host = "null";
    if(typeof url == "undefined"|| null == url){
    url = window.location.href;
    }
    var regex = /.*\:\/\/([^\/]*).*/;
    var match = url.match(regex);
    if(typeof match != "undefined"&& null != match){
        host = match[1];
    }
    return host;
}
function setCookie(name,value,expires,path,domain,secure)
{
    var liveDate = new Date();
    //expires = liveDate.setTime(liveDate.getTime() + expires*60*1000);//毫秒
    expires = new Date((new Date()).getTime() + expires * 86400000);//按天
    document.cookie = name + "=" + escape (value) +
    ((expires) ? "; expires=" + expires : "") +
    ((path) ? "; path=" + path : "") +
    ((domain) ? "; domain=" + domain : "") +
    ((secure) ? "; secure" : "");
}

function get_uname(str,len, ae) {
    var tl = 0, ts = [];
    var tt = str.length;
    for (var i = 0; i < tt; i++) {
        if (str.charCodeAt(i) > 255) {
            tl += 2;
        } else {
            tl++;
        }
        if (tl > len) {
            break;
        }
    }
    return (ae && i < tt) ? str.substring(0, i) + '...' : str.substring(0, i);
}

window.addEvent('domready',function(e){
	$ES('.miniCart').addEvent('mouseenter', function(){
		this.addClass('cur');

	MiniCarWidgets={
		init:function(){
			var minicart_detail=this.detailbox=$E('.MiniCarDetail');
			var handle=this.handle=$ES('.miniCart');
			this.attach();
		},
		load:function(options){
			this.request(options).chain(function(){

				//this.scroll().show();
			}.bind(this));
		},
		attach:function(){
			this.handle.addEvents({
				'mouseenter':function(e){
					e.stop();
					if(this.state||!Cookie.get('S[CART_NUMBER]'))return;
					this.request([{url:'http://www.s.cn/cart-cartList.html', method:'post'}]);
					this.show();
				}.bind(this),
				'mouseleave': function(e){
					this.movestate=false;
					this.hide.delay(200,this);
	            }.bind(this)
			});
			this.detailbox.addEvents({
				'mouseenter':function(e){
					this.movestate=true;
				}.bind(this),
				'mouseleave': function(e) {
					this.movestate=false;
					this.hide();
	            }.bind(this)
			});
			//this.detailbox.addEvent('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();})
		},
		show:function(e){
			this.detailbox.setStyles({'visibility':'visible','opacity':'0'}).fade('in');
			this.state=true;
			document.addEvent('click',function(){
				  this.hide();
                  document.removeEvent('click',arguments.callee);
		    }.bind(this));
		},
		scroll:function(container){
			window.scrollTo(0,this.detailbox.getPosition().y-30);
			return this;
		},
		hide:function(){
			if(this.movestate)return;
			this.state=false;
			this.detailbox.setStyle('visibility','hidden');
		},
		removeCart:function(el,type){
			if(type=='f'){
				var url='http://www.s.cn/cart-f-remove_miniCart.html';
				el.getParent('.mini_cart_list_f').remove();
			}else if(type=='r'){
				var url='http://www.s.cn/cart-r-remove_miniCart.html';
				el.getParent('.mini_cart_list_r').remove();
			}else{
				var url='http://www.s.cn/cart-g-remove_miniCart.html';
				el.getParent('.mini_cart_list_g').remove();
			}
			this.request([{url:url,data:this.detailbox,onSuccess:function(re){
				$$('.cart-num').set('text',Cookie.get('S[CART_NUMBER]')||0);
				$('totalp').set('text',re);
				MessageBox.success('删除成功');
				this.addEvent();
			}.bind(this)}]);
		},
		addEvent:function(){
			var _this=this;
			this.detailbox.getElements('.delcart_g').addEvent('click',function(e){
				e.stop();
				_this.removeCart(this,'g');
			});
			this.detailbox.getElements('.delcart_f').addEvent('click',function(e){
				e.stop();
				_this.removeCart(this,'f');
			});
			this.detailbox.getElements('.delcart_r').addEvent('click',function(e){
				e.stop();
				_this.removeCart(this,'r');
			});
			this.detailbox.addEvent('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();});	 
		},
		request:function(){
			var params=Array.flatten(arguments).link({

                 'options':Object.type
            });

					 this.addEvent();
                 }.bind(this)
             },params.options||{});
             return new Request(params).send();
		}
	};

function marquee(height,speed,delay){
var scrollT;
var pause = false;
var ScrollBox = document.getElementById("shangfan");
if(document.getElementById("holder").offsetHeight <= height) return;
var _tmp = ScrollBox.innerHTML.replace('holder', 'holder2')
ScrollBox.innerHTML += _tmp;
ScrollBox.onmouseover = function(){pause = true}
ScrollBox.onmouseout = function(){pause = false}
ScrollBox.scrollTop = 0;
function start(){
     scrollT = setInterval(scrolling,speed);
     if(!pause) ScrollBox.scrollTop += 2;
}
function scrolling(){
     if(ScrollBox.scrollTop % height != 0){
         ScrollBox.scrollTop += 2;
         if(ScrollBox.scrollTop >= ScrollBox.scrollHeight/2) ScrollBox.scrollTop = 0;
     }
   else{
         clearInterval(scrollT);
         setTimeout(start,delay);
     }
}
setTimeout(start,delay);
}
marquee(20,30,3000);

function tips_pop() {
	var MsgPop = document.getElementById("floatad-winpop");
	var popH = parseInt(MsgPop.style.height);
	if (popH == 0) {
		MsgPop.style.display = "block";
		show = setInterval("changeH('up')", 2);
	} else {
		hide = setInterval("changeH('down')", 2);
	}
}
function changeH(str) {
	var MsgPop = document.getElementById("floatad-winpop");
	var popH = parseInt(MsgPop.style.height);
	if (str == "up") {
		if (popH <= 213) {
			MsgPop.style.height = (popH + 4).toString() + "px";
		} else {
			clearInterval(show);
		}
	}
	if (str == "down") {
		if (popH >= 4) {
			MsgPop.style.height = (popH - 4).toString() + "px";
		} else {
			clearInterval(hide);
			MsgPop.style.display = "none";
		}
	}
}

window.addEvent('domready',function(){

        var forInit = $$('img[init_src]');
        var win = window;
        
        (function(){
            if(!forInit.length)return false;
            var loop = arguments.callee;
            var loop = function(){
                forInit.each(function(item,index){
                    if(!item)return;
                    if(item.getPosition(win).y>0 &&((item.getPosition(win).y-win.getScrollTop())<win.getSize().y)){
                        if(item.get('init_src')){
                            item.set('src',item.get('init_src')).removeProperty('init_src')
                        }
                        // forInit.erase(item);
                    }
                    
                    if(index == (forInit.length-1)){loop.delay(200);}
                   
                });
            }
            loop.delay(200);
        })();

});
</script> <script>
window.addEvent('domready',function(){

        var forInit = $$('img[init_src]');
        var win = this;
        
        (function(){
            if(!forInit.length)return false;
            var loop = arguments.callee;
            var loop = function(){
                forInit.each(function(item,index){
                    if(!item)return;
                    if(item.getPosition(win).y>0 &&((item.getPosition(win).y-win.getScrollTop())<win.getSize().y)){
                        if(item.get('init_src')){
                            item.set('src',item.get('init_src')).removeProperty('init_src')
                        }
                        // forInit.erase(item);
                    }
                    
                    if(index == (forInit.length-1)){loop.delay(200);}
                   
                });
            }
            loop.delay(200);
        })();

});
</script></body> </html>
